FNV PBR CONTINUITY HOT-PATH CONTRACT CLOSURE

Questions:
1. Which native PPLighting records own c32/c33, and does vanilla own c89/c90 at all?
2. When are those records applied relative to SetShaders, draw dispatch, and the next native constant update?
3. Does any engine D3D SetTexture path bypass NiDX9RenderState::SetTexture?
4. Can Begin/End/CreateStateBlock or another direct D3D path change textures without that hook?
5. Is there a direct current pass-entry bridge, or what exact selector/property/pass key can cache ownership?
6. Which functions build, mutate, clear, or invalidate selector +0x3C entries and property +0x38/+0x74 state?

The script uses exact callsite argument and virtual-call patterns. A method displacement alone still does not prove the receiver interface.

======================================================================
CONSTANT-TABLE REGISTER COVERAGE
======================================================================
The +0x08 interface method receives name, type, selector, register start, and register count as its first five arguments.
Coverage below is numeric only. Vertex/pixel ownership must be resolved from the enclosing table constructor stage.
